Denies any fever, chills, cough or shortness of breath. He has been eating and drinking fairly well. He has been maintaining his weight. He actually had moved with his daughter at the time of his neutropenia and is currently staying with her.   FAMILY HISTORY: No change.   SOCIAL HISTORY: No change.   CURRENT MEDICATIONS: Reviewed and updated in --- Company ---. Specifically, he is taking Levaquin 500 mg a day, acyclovir 400 mg 3 times a day, Noxafil has been on hold because of the recent vincristine. Rest of his medications were updated.   PHYSICAL EXAMINATION: GENERAL: The patient is a leanly built male in no obvious distress. VITAL SIGNS: Noted and within normal limits. He is afebrile. HEENT: Sclerae is anicteric, not pale. HEENT is within normal limits. There is no mucositis. There is no thrush. NECK: Supple. Trachea is central. Thyroid gland is not palpable. LUNGS: Clear. HEART: Heart sounds are normal. ABDOMEN: Soft, nontender. EXTREMITIES: No cyanosis, clubbing or edema. There is no skin rash.   LABORATORY DATA: Lab tests done today reveals a white count of 2400, hemoglobin of 8.9 and platelet count of 52,000. Absolute neutrophil count: Segs 63%, bands 9%, lymphs 14, monos 10 and basophils 3. Chemistry reveals a BUN of 8, creatinine of 0.83 and albumin of 3.2.   PROBLEMS:  1. Mantle cell lymphoma. The patient is currently day #14, status post third cycle of chemotherapy. He has already recovered his counts. In this regard, we are planning to give him rituximab early next week and he will be admitted for the fourth cycle of chemotherapy which will be high-dose methotrexate and cytarabine in the early part right after --- Date ---. This was discussed with the patient and he is agreeable.  2. Infectious disease. There is no active infection. He is on prophylactic Levaquin and acyclovir. Since his counts have recovered, prophylatic Levaquin can be stopped right now. He will be taking his Noxafil as scheduled with keeping his interaction with vincristine in place. He was due to start with that today, which would have been about 72 hours from the last dose of vincristine.  3. Regimen-related <ADE>toxicity</ADE></ADVERSE>  that has been none. There has not been
